We come here because they are located a few blocks away from our home. As someone that has been in the customer service industry for the past 20 years I can say that  the staff at this establishment should be replace for someone that is capable of helping their customers.
I'm not going to elaborate on the terrible experience but I will share with you that only a couple of miles south Enterprise Car Rental had me driving one of their cars within minutes for a lot less money.
It was the night and day difference in service provided by these two establishments that convinced me to write this review. Rude service will never make happy customers, I don't care for your cheap suits and poor service. I hope this helps you change your attitude towards customers.</review>

10/4/18 - Happy Hour at Heritage Fine Wines in  Beverly Hills.

Happy HOURS:  Mon - Fri, 5-7pm
* my visit: Thursday at 6:40pm, party of 3

Happy Hour MENU:
â€¢ Wine selection is quite limited, offering only 5 wines of which there are 2 sparkling, 1 rose, 1 red, and 1 white. Wine prices are fair ranging $8-$12 per glass. Average/normal wine pours.

â€¢ Food options are cheese, meat, bruschetta and tapenades, and oysters. The prices range from $5-$18. Its a good spread of finger-sized foods to share between 2-3 ppl.

* our order (3ppl):  Sparkling Rose, Rose, and Bordeaux (my fav!) and to eat we had the 3pc Bruschetta and Tapenade (my fav!). Our total bill came to $44.85 (w/o tip), which in my opinion was a rather reasonable.

SERVICE:  the staff was friendly but the the service was quite slow, having to get up from the table and walk to the bar twice to ask for another drink and silverware, as well as trying to track someone down for the check.

ATMOSPHERE & AMBIANCE:  the restaurant/bar looks upscale, and had a warm cozy feel with dim lighting and candles set atop wine barrels. There was a piano player in the back to set them mood. It seems to cater to an older, more mature crowd in the age range of mid-30â€™s and up.

There is a good amount of seating throughout the restaurant and they were placed in a way to avoid overcrowding and to give each party there one sense of personal space. The seating options were bar seats (approx 8-10), 2 high top tables (each seats approx 4-6), and several regular tables at the center of the restaurant (from what I saw it looked like the tables could accommodate 2-8ppl/table).

Iâ€™ve passed by this place countless number of times over the years and had always wanted to go in and Iâ€™m glad I finally did. I will certainly go back soon.<//Review>

< text>
Great ice cream, friendly service
This tiny ice cream shop has been at Tower Park for several years. The people that run it are owner-operators. She personally makes all of the baked goods, including cookies, brownies, waffle cones, etc. They serve Gunther's ice cream (from Sacramento) and it's delicious. The only drawback is that it's a small shop so they have only 10 flavors. But they're all wonderful!< /text>

<Text>Great place to watch local theater.  In the main stage, rows A, C and K are a bit higher than the other rows. Row J is the first row J of the second section and it's ok, but foot traffic can be an issue. This place also has two bathrooms for women and one for men. You can bring food and drink into the theater, but they ask that you don't eat during the show. On street parking is plentiful, but the city aggressively tickets.  Large parking lot just across from theater. TV in the lounge area displaying show in real time so you don't miss a scene.</Text><time>1512876269607< /time></record>

< Review>

Wonder filled evening! We attended an opening night event in the main theater. Arrived early for the pre-show talk. The executive director is hilariously funny. The venue is cozy and you can see well from every seat. There's a good reason this company has been delivering theatre for 75 years. Parking is easy. The location is easy to get to. There is good dining all around. Treat yourself to an evening on the town. I doubt you could do better than this.</Review>

<Text>This place was packed with people trying to escape the heat of summer. The line was out the door but the blast of the cool AC air once you step inside made the wait totally worth it. The place was filled with kids, the elderly, families, and everyone in between. It definitely felt like organized chaos but with a very relaxed vibe. <user>111786517743281339317</user><user_name>Tiffany C</user_name><Date>1463293764064</Date><Rate>3< /Rate><Review>Apparently It's Boba Time is a pretty popular boba joint in the LA area. I honestly don't think it can compare to the plethora of boba shops littered around SGV ... at all. I would say It's Boba Time is a mix of Quickly's and Tapioca Express on a slightly higher level.

They specialize in pretty much everything and anything. If you are craving it, they probably have it. This extensive menu is probably why they have a ton of workers in the kitchen, pushing out drinks like there's no tomorrow. I feel like they should condense their menu and just stick to what they're more known for ... but of course, my opinion doesn't matter.

This location is also pretty hard to find parking. The lot is tiny, it's hard to get in and out when traffic is super busy, and if there's a line out the door ... I don't know if it's worth it to stop for boba - and this is coming from me, a boba fanatic.

It's quite interesting to see the many different people coming in to enjoy boba. In the SGV, these shops are typically crowded with Asians, but it's really nice to see all kinds of people at It's Boba Time. Made me curious as I wanted to see what they ordered, but their drinks were way fancier than I had expected.

I ordered a simple green tea with boba. I believe boba was a free add-on ... and who can turn down free boba?! Price was not too bad. I think it was a tad bit more than what I would probably pay for the drink, but overall the tea was pretty expected, and also pretty standard of a drink I'd get at Quickly's. Tea tasted good, but did not taste like premium tea; rather, it was a bit on the artificial side. The boba was cooked pretty well. Super chewy, which I liked.

Even with the long line, I had to commend the workers on how quickly they pushed the orders out. Will I be returning here for boba? Ha, no - especially not when I can go to one of the many places in 626 and get tastier drinks. But if I was ever in the neighborhood and the parking lot was empty and there isn't a ton of traffic on Vermont, I could see myself coming back.</Review><Pictures>None< /Pictures><Resp>None</Resp>< gmap_id>
